    <script>

      var utmContent = null;
      var utmSource = null;
      var shareEventId = null;

      window.onpageshow = function(event) {
        $('#loading').hide();
      };

      $( document ).ready(function() {
        if (window.innerWidth < 330){
          document.documentElement.style.zoom = "0.8"
        }

        // 페이지 로드시에도 이미지 업데이트를 위해 호출
        let screenWidth = window.innerWidth;

        var temp_banner = document.getElementById('event-banner-img');
        var pcImgUrl = temp_banner.getAttribute('data-pc');
        var mobileImgUrl = temp_banner.getAttribute('data-mobile');

        if (screenWidth >= 500){
          temp_banner.src = pcImgUrl
        } else {
          temp_banner.src = mobileImgUrl
        }

        window.addEventListener('resize', changeImage);

        //1시간을 나타낸다
        const date = new Date()
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + 60 * 60 * 1000)
        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

        utmContent = urlParams.get('utm_content');
        utmSource = urlParams.get('utm_source')
        if (utmContent){
          if (getCookie('utm_content') == null){
            document.cookie = 'utm_content='+utmContent+';expires='+date+';'
          }
        }

        if (utmSource){
          if (getCookie('utm_source') == null){
            document.cookie = 'utm_source='+utmSource+';expires='+date+';'
          }
        }

        shareEventId = urlParams.get("share_event_id");
        // 5분을 셋팅해준다.
        const shareDate = new Date()
        shareDate.setTime(shareDate.getTime() + 60 * 5 * 1000)
        if (shareEventId){
          if (getCookie("share_event_id") == null){
            // 기존 것은 지우고 다시 셋팅해준다.
            document.cookie = "share_event_id="+shareEventId+';expires='+shareDate+';'
          }
        }

        $("input#search_input").on("focus", function() {
          $(this).attr("placeholder", "");
        });

        document.getElementById('form_submit').addEventListener('submit', function(event) {
          // var input_value = document.getElementById('search_input').value;
          // new_event. 상품 검색이 발생하는 순간
          var currentUrl = window.location.href;
          var temp_search_event_name = ''
          if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')){
            temp_search_event_name = 'product_page_searched'
          } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')){
            temp_search_event_name = 'search_page_searched'
          } else {
            temp_search_event_name = 'main_page_searched'
          }

          fbq('trackCustom', temp_search_event_name);
          gtag("event", temp_search_event_name);
          $('#loading').show();
        });

        // new_event. 웹사이트내 모든 웹 페이지에 페이지 로드가 발생하는 순간
        fbq("trackCustom", "page_viewed");
        gtag("event", "page_viewed");

        var currentUrl = window.location.href;
        var event_name = 'hej_web_main_imp'
        if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')){
            event_name = 'hej_web_detail_imp'
        } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')){
          event_name = 'hej_web_search_imp'
        }

        gtag("event", event_name);

        // 카카오 픽셀 설치
        kakaoPixel('4166971727777215001').pageView();

      function changeImage(){
        let screenWidth = window.innerWidth;

        var temp_banner = document.getElementById('event-banner-img');
        var pcImgUrl = temp_banner.getAttribute('data-pc');
        var mobileImgUrl = temp_banner.getAttribute('data-mobile');

        if (screenWidth >= 500){
          temp_banner.src = pcImgUrl
        } else {
          temp_banner.src = mobileImgUrl
        }

      }
      function getCookie(name) {
        const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
        const parts = value.split(`; ${name}=`);
        if (parts.length === 2) return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
      }

      function modal_show() {
        document.querySelector(".modal_background").className = "modal_background modal_show";
      }

      function modal_close() {
        document.querySelector(".modal_background").className = "modal_background";
      }

      function copy_down_url(){
        if ($(".modal_background").css('z-index')=="1000"){
          // id가 qrcode_img의 alt를 가져온다.
          let elementText = document.getElementById('qrcode_img').alt;

          navigator.clipboard.writeText(elementText).then(function(x){
          alert("앱 다운로드 URL이 복사되었어요!")
          })
        }
      }

      function get_app_down_url(from_where){

        // 신규버전은 from_where이 있다.
        if (from_where){
          var app_down_url = "";
          var app_down_qr = "";
          if (from_where === 'main_floating'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/qrvoxf"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/main_floating_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'footer_appstore'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/wbehrr"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/footer_appstore_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'footer_playstore'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/odwepg"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/footer_playstore_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'footer_app_download'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/hmoymq"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/footer_app_download_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'detail_graph'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/vd5hyx"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/detail_graph_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'detail_bottom'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/x8zfbn"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/detail_bottom_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'main_bottom_floating'){
            app_down_url = "https://abr.ge/smgonz"
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/main_bottom_floating_qr.png"
          } else if (from_where === 'main_rolling'){
            app_down_url = 'https://abr.ge/oghm2g'
            app_down_qr = "https://fallcent-image.s3.amazonaws.com/product/main_rolling_qr.png"
          }

          // id가 qrcode_img의 src에 app_down_qr을 넣어준다.
          document.getElementById('qrcode_img').src = app_down_qr;
          // id가 qrcode_img의 alt에 app_down_url을 넣어준다.
          document.getElementById('qrcode_img').alt = app_down_url;

          return app_down_url;
        }

        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        // utmContent = urlParams.get('utm_content') || getCookie("utm_content") || null;
        utmSource = urlParams.get('utm_source') || getCookie("utm_source") || null;

        // 메인, 상세, 검색을 모두 나눈다.
        const currentUrl = window.location.href;

        // 기존 것을 사용
        var app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/71ieobqj"

        if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')){
          if (utmSource){
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/jhoigh8e"
          } else {
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/dff5v6oy"
          }
        } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')){
          if (utmSource){
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/jhoigh8e"
          } else {
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/dff5v6oy"
          }
        } else {
          if (utmSource){
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/h3anuye0"
          } else {
            app_down_url = "https://fallcent.onelink.me/q8W4/6tcyeuq0"
          }
        }

        return app_down_url
      }

      function clickAppDownButton(event_name){
        // 메인, 상세, 검색을 모두 나눈다.
        const currentUrl = window.location.href;

        // 일단 플루팅부터 나눈다.
        var new_event_name = event_name
        if (event_name === 'plot_app_download'){
          if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')){
            new_event_name = 'product_plot_app_download_clicked'
          } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')){
            new_event_name = 'search_plot_app_download_clicked'
          } else {
            new_event_name = 'main_plot_app_download_clicked'
          }
        } else if (event_name === 'bottom_app_download') {
          if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')) {
            new_event_name = 'product_bottom_app_download_clicked'
          } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')) {
            new_event_name = 'search_bottom_app_download_clicked'
          } else {
            new_event_name = 'main_bottom_app_download_clicked'
          }
        }

        // fbq("trackCustom", "app_down_button_"+utmContent);
        // fbq("trackCustom", "app_down_button");
        fbq("trackCustom", new_event_name);
        fbq("track", "CompleteRegistration");
        gtag("event", new_event_name);
        // 카카오 이벤트 추가
        kakaoPixel('4166971727777215001').signUp();

        <!-- 네이버 디스플레이 광고 -->
        var _nasa={};
        if (window.wcs) {
          _nasa["cnv"] = wcs.cnv("4","1");
          wcs_do(_nasa);
        }

        if (shareEventId){
          send_share_event(shareEventId, "click_app_down_button");
        }

        if (/Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) { // Mobile
          // var app_url = "";
          // // 모바일일 때는 plot_app_download가 다르게 처리한다.
          // if (event_name === 'plot_app_download'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('main_bottom_floating')
          // } else if (event_name === 'bottom_app_download'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('footer_app_download')
          // } else if (event_name === 'bottom_appstore'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('footer_appstore')
          // } else if (event_name === 'bottom_playstore'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('footer_playstore')
          // } else if (event_name === 'chart_down_click'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('detail_graph')
          // } else if (event_name === 'product_alarm_clicked'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('detail_bottom')
          // } else if (event_name === 'main_hotdeal_last_downloaded_clicked'){
          //   app_url = get_app_down_url('main_rolling')
          // }
          // window.open(app_url, "_self")
        } else {
          // PC 우측 플루팅 버튼
          if (event_name === 'plot_app_download'){
            get_app_down_url('main_floating')
          } else if (event_name === 'bottom_app_download'){
            get_app_down_url('footer_app_download')
          } else if (event_name === 'bottom_appstore'){
            get_app_down_url('footer_appstore')
          } else if (event_name === 'bottom_playstore'){
            get_app_down_url('footer_playstore')
          } else if (event_name === 'chart_down_click'){
            get_app_down_url('detail_graph')
          } else if (event_name === 'product_alarm_clicked'){
            get_app_down_url('detail_bottom')
          } else if (event_name === 'main_hotdeal_last_downloaded_clicked'){
            get_app_down_url('main_rolling')
          }
          modal_show()
        }
      }


      function click_popular_keyword(keyword){
        // event3. 인기검색어 클릭 / popular_keyword_clicked / keyword
        // fbq('trackCustom', 'popular_keyword_clicked', {keyword: keyword});
        $('#loading').show();

      }

      function click_product(product_id, item_id){
        // event3. 상품 클릭 / product_clicked / product_id, item_id
        // fbq('trackCustom', 'product_clicked', {product_id:product_id, item_id:item_id});
        $('#loading').show();
      }

      function click_event_banner(){
        const currentUrl = window.location.href;
        var event_name = 'hej_web_main_click'
        if (currentUrl.includes('product/?')) {
          event_name = 'hej_web_detail_click'
        } else if (currentUrl.includes('product/search')) {
          event_name = 'hej_web_search_click'
        }

        gtag("event", event_name);
      }


      function introduction_clicked(){
        // new_event13. 폴센트 소개버튼 클릭 / introduction_clicked / product_id, item_id
        fbq('trackCustom', 'introduced_clicked');
        gtag("event", "introduced_clicked");
      }

      function onBackButton(){
        window.history.back();
      }

      function send_share_event(share_event_id, status){
        <!-- 링크 클릭 , 구매하러 가기 클릭 , 앱 다운로드 클릭 3개 이벤트 보내주기-->
        var data ={
          "share_event_id" : share_event_id,
          "status" : status,
        };

        $.ajax({
          type: "GET",
          url: "https://fallcent.com/api/v5/fallcent/api/event/share/web/",
          data : data,
          contentType : "application/json; charset=utf-8",
          error: function() {
            console.log('통신실패!!');
          },
          success: function(data) {
            console.log('통신성공!!');
          }
        });
      }

      
    var beforeClick = "#전체"
    var slides;
    var indicators;
    let currentSlide = 0;
    let startX;

    $( document ).ready(function() {
      // 전체 부분은 보이도록 한다.
      $(beforeClick).css("display", "")
      var element = document.getElementById("category_전체");
      element.classList.remove("category_color")
      element.classList.add("click_category")

      <!-- utm 파악하기 -->
      var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      var utmContent = urlParams.get('utm_content') || getCookie("utm_content") || 1;
      fbq("trackCustom", "main_page_viewed_"+utmContent);
      fbq("trackCustom", "main_page_viewed");
      gtag("event", "main_page_viewed");


      slides = document.querySelector('.slides');
      indicators = document.querySelectorAll('.indicator');

      indicators.forEach((indicator, index) => {
        indicator.addEventListener('click', () => showSlide(index));
      });

      document.querySelector('.prev').addEventListener('click', prevSlide);
      document.querySelector('.next').addEventListener('click', nextSlide);

      slides.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
        startX = e.touches[0].pageX;
      });

      slides.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
        const x = e.changedTouches[0].pageX;
        const diff = startX - x;

        if (diff > 10) {
          nextSlide();
        } else if (diff < -10) {
          prevSlide();
        }
        startX = null;
      });

      setChart();

      <!-- 첫번 째 인디케이터 -->
      showSlide(0);

      <!-- 에어브릿지 이벤트 전송 -->
      airbridge.events.send('airbridge.ecommerce.home.viewed')

      <!-- 에어브릿지 cta이벤트 롤링 끝부분-->
      airbridge.setDeeplinks({
          buttonID: "main_hotdeal_last_downloaded_clicked",
          deeplinks: {
            ios: "fallcent://",
            android: "fallcent://",
          },
          fallbacks: {
            ios: "itunes-appstore",
            android: "google-play"
          },
          defaultParams: {
            campaign: 'example_campaign',
            medium: 'example_medium',
            term: 'example_term',
            content: 'example_content'
          },
          ctaParams: {
            cta_param_1: 'main',
            cta_param_2: 'rolling_install_all',
            cta_param_3: 'main_rolling',
          },
          desktopPopUp: false  // 이것은 새창을 띄울지 말지를 결정합니다.
      });
    });

    function click_category(category) {
      var elements = document.getElementsByClassName("click_category"); // click_keyword 클래스를 가진 모든 요소를 선택합니다.
      for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
        elements[i].classList.remove("click_category"); // click_keyword 클래스를 제외합니다.
      }

      var temp_category = "category_"+category
      var element = document.getElementById(temp_category);
      if (element != null) {
        element.classList.add("click_category")
        element.classList.remove("category_color")
      }
      // 이제 급락한 상품들 부분에서 있던 상품들을 다 지워주고, append해주자.
      $(beforeClick).css("display", "none")
      beforeClick = "#" + category.replace("/", "\\/")
      $(beforeClick).css("display", "")
    }

    function showSlide(index) {
      slides.style.transform = `translateX(-${index * 100}%)`;
      indicators.forEach((indicator, i) => {
        indicator.classList.toggle('active', i === index);
      });
      currentSlide = index;
    }

    function nextSlide() {
      currentSlide = (currentSlide + 1) % indicators.length;
      showSlide(currentSlide);
    }

    function prevSlide() {
      currentSlide = (currentSlide - 1 + indicators.length) % indicators.length;
      showSlide(currentSlide);
    }

      var hot_deal_product_chart = JSON.parse(test);
      for (i = 0 ; i < hot_deal_product_chart.length; i ++ ){

          chart_info = hot_deal_product_chart[i];
          const ctx = document.getElementById('priceChart_'+chart_info["product_id"]);
          var context = ctx.getContext('2d');

          // no we get with of content and asign the same hight as the with. this gives up aspect ration 1:1.
          context.canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
          if (window.innerWidth < 500){
            context.canvas.height = window.innerWidth / 1.7;
          } else {
            context.canvas.height = window.innerWidth / 2.2;
          }

          const labels = chart_info['date_list']
          const data = {
            labels: labels,
            datasets: [
              {
                label: '최저가',
                data: chart_info['lowest_price_list'],
                borderColor: '#F56666',
                backgroundColor: '#F56666',
                pointRadius: 0,
                borderWidth: 2,
                borderJoinStyle: 'round',
              },
             {
                label: '최고가',
                data: chart_info['highest_price_list'],
                borderColor: '#14AF40',
                backgroundColor: '#14AF40',
                yAxisID: 'y',
                pointRadius: 0,
                borderWidth: 2,
                borderJoinStyle: 'round',
              },
            ]
          };
          const config = {
            type: 'line',
            data: data,
            options: {
              responsive: true,
              interaction: {
                mode: 'index',
                intersect: false,
              },
              stacked: false,
              plugins: {
                title: {
                  display: false,
                  text: '가격 그래프'
                },
                legend: {
                  position: 'top',
                  align: 'end',
                },
              },
              scales: {
                x: {
                  grid: {
                    display: false, // x 축의 그리드를 숨깁니다.
                  },
                },
                y: {
                  type: 'linear',
                  display: true,
                  position: 'left',
                },
                y1: {
                  type: 'linear',
                  display: false,
                  position: 'right',
                  // grid line settings
                  grid: {
                    drawOnChartArea: true, // only want the grid lines for one axis to show up
                  },
                },
              }
            },
          };

          const myChart = new Chart(ctx, config);

      }

    }
